***устроить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a> (1216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stroitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustróitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arrange, to organize, to establish</li>
<li>to settle, to set up, to put in order</li>
<li>to suit, to satisfy</li></ol>

***устроиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́иться</a> (2713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustróitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраиваться.html>устра́иваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle down, to get settled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́иться</a></b> поудо́бнее</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustróitʹsja</b> poudóbneje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make oneself comfortable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́иться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustróitʹsja</b> na rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get fixed up in a job, to get a job</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn out right, to get fine, to be OK
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́йся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́ится</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne bespokójsja, máma, vsjó <b>ustróitsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't worry, mum, everything will be OK (will come out alright).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступать.html>уступа́емый</a> (4335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступать.html>уступа́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustupájemyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступать.html>уступа́ть</a> (4335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступать.html>уступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<dl><dd><i>(object in the accusative case, receiver in the dative case)</i></dd></dl>
<ol><li>to cede, to let have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступи́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustupíli zemli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They ceded ground.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to yield</li>
<li>to be inferior to <i>(+ dative case)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>усту́пит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nikomú ne ustúpit v étom otnošénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is second to none in this regard.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reduce something as part of agreement</li>
<li>to discount, to abate, to reduce price
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>усту́пят</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:копейка.html>копе́йки</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní ne ustúpjat ni kopéjki!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They won’t take one cent less!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступлю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vam ustupljú knígu rubléj za dvésti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ll let you have the book for around two hundred roubles.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступить.html>ступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступать.html>уступа́ть</a></b>) <i>(object in the accusative case, receiver in the dative case)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to cede</li>
<li>to let have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступлю́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vam <b>ustupljú</b> knígu rubléj za dvésti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ll let you have the book for around two hundred roubles.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to yield</li>
<li>to be inferior to <i>(+ dative case)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>усту́пит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nikomú ne <b>ustúpit</b> v étom otnošénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is second to none in this regard.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sell</li>
<li>to discount, to abate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>усту́пят</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:копейка.html>копе́йки</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní ne <b>ustúpjat</b> ni kopéjki!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They won’t take one cent less!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступчивый.html>усту́пчивый</a> (31918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чивый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уступчивый.html>усту́пчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustúpčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>amenable, conciliatory, compromising

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стье</a> (8766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ústʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стий</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устье.html>у́стьев</a></b>)

***усугубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усугубить.html>усугубить</a> (26162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сугу́бый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sugúbyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усугубить.html>усугуби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usugubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усугублять.html>усугубля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to redouble, to intensify, to increase, to aggravate</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:су.html>су</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́б</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лён<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/b(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-сугубл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ённ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***усыновить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усыновить.html>усынови́ть</a> (19570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыновить.html>усынови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usynovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">усыновля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to adopt, to affiliate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to take by choice into relationship as child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The term is derived from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">syn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">son</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, so originally it meant to make someone one's son. It is also used as a generic term for adoption. To refer to female adoption specifically, use <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удочери́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udočerítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усыновить.html>усынови́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — усыновлять.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-сын-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ов-и</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usypítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́вший</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>--</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́ть</a> (15409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сыпи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sypítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, causative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съпати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭpati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъpati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usypítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыплять.html>усыпля́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to allay (suspicions)</li>
<li>to euthanize (an animal)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usypítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыплять.html>усыпля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">usypljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усыпить.html>усыпи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put/lull to sleep</li>
<li>to allay (suspicions)</li>
<li>to euthanize (an animal)</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make off <i>(with)</i>, to steal</li></ol>
